## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Environment {
        +String name: dev2
        +List~Cluster~ clusters
        +Role role
    }
    class Cluster {
        +String name
        +String endpoint
        +String ca
        +String deployment
    }
    class Role {
        +String arn
    }
    class GreenCluster {
        +name: fv-vpc-001-dev2-eks-green
        +deployment: green
        +endpoint: ref+awssecrets://dev2/eks/greenConfig#endpoint
        +ca: ref+awssecrets://dev2/eks/greenConfig#ca
    }
    class BlueCluster {
        +name: fv-vpc-001-dev2-eks-blue
        +deployment: blue
        +endpoint: ref+awssecrets://dev2/eks/blueConfig#endpoint
        +ca: ref+awssecrets://dev2/eks/blueConfig#ca
    }
    Environment "1" --> "2" Cluster
    Environment "1" --> "1" Role
    Cluster <|-- GreenCluster
    Cluster <|-- BlueCluster
```
